\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{lib_2function__base_8py_source_l02602}02602\ \textcolor{stringliteral}{\ \ \ \ steps\ to\ compute\ the\ weighted\ covariance\ are\ as\ follows::}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{lib_2function__base_8py_source_l02603}02603\ \textcolor{stringliteral}{}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{lib_2function__base_8py_source_l02604}02604\ \textcolor{stringliteral}{\ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ >>>\ m\ =\ np.arange(10,\ dtype=np.float64)}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{lib_2function__base_8py_source_l02605}02605\ \textcolor{stringliteral}{\ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ >>>\ f\ =\ np.arange(10)\ *\ 2}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{lib_2function__base_8py_source_l02606}02606\ \textcolor{stringliteral}{\ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ >>>\ a\ =\ np.arange(10)\ **\ 2.}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{lib_2function__base_8py_source_l02607}02607\ \textcolor{stringliteral}{\ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ >>>\ ddof\ =\ 1}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{lib_2function__base_8py_source_l02608}02608\ \textcolor{stringliteral}{\ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ >>>\ w\ =\ f\ *\ a}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{lib_2function__base_8py_source_l02609}02609\ \textcolor{stringliteral}{\ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ >>>\ v1\ =\ np.sum(w)}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{lib_2function__base_8py_source_l02610}02610\ \textcolor{stringliteral}{\ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ >>>\ v2\ =\ np.sum(w\ *\ a)}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{lib_2function__base_8py_source_l02611}02611\ \textcolor{stringliteral}{\ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ >>>\ m\ -\/=\ np.sum(m\ *\ w,\ axis=None,\ keepdims=True)\ /\ v1}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{lib_2function__base_8py_source_l02612}02612\ \textcolor{stringliteral}{\ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ >>>\ cov\ =\ np.dot(m\ *\ w,\ m.T)\ *\ v1\ /\ (v1**2\ -\/\ ddof\ *\ v2)}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{lib_2function__base_8py_source_l02613}02613\ \textcolor{stringliteral}{}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{lib_2function__base_8py_source_l02614}02614\ \textcolor{stringliteral}{\ \ \ \ Note\ that\ when\ \`{}\`{}a\ ==\ 1\`{}\`{},\ the\ normalization\ factor}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{lib_2function__base_8py_source_l02615}02615\ \textcolor{stringliteral}{\ \ \ \ \`{}\`{}v1\ /\ (v1**2\ -\/\ ddof\ *\ v2)\`{}\`{}\ goes\ over\ to\ \`{}\`{}1\ /\ (np.sum(f)\ -\/\ ddof)\`{}\`{}}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{lib_2function__base_8py_source_l02616}02616\ \textcolor{stringliteral}{\ \ \ \ as\ it\ should.}}
